      <div class="main section" id="main">
       <div class="widget Blog" id="Blog1">
        <div class="blog-posts hfeed">
         <!-- google_ad_section_start(name=default) -->
         <div class="date-outer">
          <h2 class="date-header">
           <span>
            Thursday, March 8, 2012
           </span>
          </h2>
          <div class="date-posts">
           <div class="post-outer">
            <div class="post hentry">
             <a name="1617849595624872440">
             </a>
             <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
              <a href="http://www.aestheticnest.com/2012/03/how-to-crochet-5-seaming-your-work.html">
               How to Crochet 5: Seaming Your Work
              </a>
             </h3>
             <div class="post-header">
              <div class="post-header-line-1">
              </div>
             </div>
             <div class="post-body entry-content">
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-UcvK_p6Lp0E/T1kzxYpetmI/AAAAAAAAKrQ/inmXZJfMFm8/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1872.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                <img border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-UcvK_p6Lp0E/T1kzxYpetmI/AAAAAAAAKrQ/inmXZJfMFm8/s800/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1872.jpg"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
               In this how-to series we could move right on from
               <a href="http://www.aestheticnest.com/2012/03/how-to-crochet-4-single-crochet.html">
                single crochet
               </a>
               to the other stitches (double crochet, half double crochet and triple crochet) but I'm pausing to talk about "seaming" because if you want to make anything other than washcloths or rectangular scarves or afghans (which are all good) you're going to need to seam some pieces together. Seaming is a good skill to have and it can be the difference between a cute sweater looking handmade instead of homemade. I am going to share two different methods. The first is the invisiblemattress stitch, which works equally well for knitting or crochet by the way, and the second seaming method uses a single crochet stitch.
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-r5l_-ceHPk0/T1lyCeOpgtI/AAAAAAAAKsE/hSwwCShfdBs/s1600/How+to+Crochet_Image_DSC_0868+copy.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                <img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-r5l_-ceHPk0/T1lyCeOpgtI/AAAAAAAAKsE/hSwwCShfdBs/s800/How+to+Crochet_Image_DSC_0868+copy.jpg" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
               Click to view the full tutorial.
              </div>
              <br/>
              <a name="more">
              </a>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Gbqw6Kv1zRM/T1pFdhdOuTI/AAAAAAAAKwg/FRbLu7WklHg/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1875.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-Gbqw6Kv1zRM/T1pFdhdOuTI/AAAAAAAAKwg/FRbLu7WklHg/s800/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1875.jpg" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <br/>
              SEAMING WITH THE MATTRESS STITCH:
              <br/>
              You will need a tapestry needle to do the seaming, which is a large blunt needle and a big eye for threading the yarn. I am going to use a contrasting yarn for this tutorial but you'll want to use the same yarn you used for your project so it blends in.
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-YTecX7ohXUM/T1kxrndoJhI/AAAAAAAAKmo/faSlhtFdDLc/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1837.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-YTecX7ohXUM/T1kxrndoJhI/AAAAAAAAKmo/faSlhtFdDLc/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1837.JPG" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <br/>
              The mattress stitch is so fabulous because it's virtually invisible if you line up the stitches correctly. If your pattern calls for "blocking" the work you will typically want to do that before seaming so the pieces all lie flat. You start with the two pieces you are joining right side up, facing you. (Crochet is often reversible, so if either side would work form a fit/pattern perspective and you don't see a visible difference, just pick one!)
              <br/>
              <br/>
              Most often you will be seaming pieces of the same length, or number of rows, so each row should line up as you go, but it's not a bad idea to use safety pins or stitch markers to line up the seam at top, bottom and a few places in between. That way you'll be sure you don't end up with a part of the seam stretched to fit.
              <br/>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-YHvUGGf1L5o/T1kxvqrbSZI/AAAAAAAAKmw/BA_fyYSqTWU/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1838.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-YHvUGGf1L5o/T1kxvqrbSZI/AAAAAAAAKmw/BA_fyYSqTWU/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1838.JPG" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               To start, cut a length of yarn about twice the length of your seam and thread your tapestry needle. No knots.
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-41TkAH39X9M/T1kxy7S3CZI/AAAAAAAAKm4/IvkccZqBUc8/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1839.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-41TkAH39X9M/T1kxy7S3CZI/AAAAAAAAKm4/IvkccZqBUc8/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1839.JPG" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               Working with the piece on the right, insert the needle from the wrong side to the right side (back to the front of the piece) in the lowermost leftstitch and pull the yarn through until you have a tail of about three or four inches for weaving in later.
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-WI0816yLfdM/T1kx2pvI2iI/AAAAAAAAKnA/VOwntUMnALw/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1840.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-WI0816yLfdM/T1kx2pvI2iI/AAAAAAAAKnA/VOwntUMnALw/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1840.JPG" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               Now insert the needle from back to front of the lefthand piece in the mirror stitch (the lowermost right corner). The key to working this seam perfectly is to mirror your stitches--working your needles in and out of the stitches on each piece in exactly the same way.
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-I1ABBx51JfA/T1kx7h_agyI/AAAAAAAAKnM/VkVhfWSRfU4/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1841.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-I1ABBx51JfA/T1kx7h_agyI/AAAAAAAAKnM/VkVhfWSRfU4/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1841.JPG" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               So you will now insert your needle through the piece on the right in that same lowermost stitch. Push the needle under to the back sideand out the next stitch up to the front side.
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-6YSfNg9vxyg/T1k6oF_wP5I/AAAAAAAAKr4/AtAa3Z7gZOY/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1842.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-6YSfNg9vxyg/T1k6oF_wP5I/AAAAAAAAKr4/AtAa3Z7gZOY/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1842.JPG" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-MyWnj3ouHfs/T1mHyoa84-I/AAAAAAAAKv8/lTqrYXu185A/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1843.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-MyWnj3ouHfs/T1mHyoa84-I/AAAAAAAAKv8/lTqrYXu185A/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1843.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div style="text-align: center;">
               Do the same (mirroring) on the left side: insert the needle in the lowermost stitch from the front to the back, up one stitch and out through the front again.
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-adT5Rl2w-4M/T1kyFhrpeyI/AAAAAAAAKno/875EIbIwDqw/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1844.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-adT5Rl2w-4M/T1kyFhrpeyI/AAAAAAAAKno/875EIbIwDqw/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1844.JPG" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               You can keep these stitches loose right now--you'll pull them tight later.
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <img border="0" height="424" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-MPPtqygSwoY/T1kyHSsmgJI/AAAAAAAAKnw/mieeN8vSbCI/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1845.JPG" width="640"/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               Continue working up your seam in this way, back and forth mirroring the same stitches on the right and left, working up one stitch (or row) at a time.
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-NwODiGpw4vQ/T1mBSNdHo6I/AAAAAAAAKsU/0KoVPSYmqcs/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1846.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-NwODiGpw4vQ/T1mBSNdHo6I/AAAAAAAAKsU/0KoVPSYmqcs/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1846.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-eRDMVnqQSSE/T1mBWprAVwI/AAAAAAAAKsc/FQK7O9ZLt-w/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1847.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-eRDMVnqQSSE/T1mBWprAVwI/AAAAAAAAKsc/FQK7O9ZLt-w/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1847.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-PreL7jEbpbo/T1mBc_SStXI/AAAAAAAAKsk/QAbAQSj7JNk/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1848.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-PreL7jEbpbo/T1mBc_SStXI/AAAAAAAAKsk/QAbAQSj7JNk/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1848.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               Every couple inches you will want to pause and pull your working yarn upin the direction of the seamto tighten the stitch.
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-J7dZ9rEFJ74/T1mSvnVGegI/AAAAAAAAKwY/_YkafAqx9XE/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1849.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-J7dZ9rEFJ74/T1mSvnVGegI/AAAAAAAAKwY/_YkafAqx9XE/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1849.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div style="text-align: center;">
               The yarnshould glide through the stitches pretty easily--be careful not to pull it all the way out.
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-D8JE_oE4V0E/T1mBoqWm3mI/AAAAAAAAKs4/q5bsK8-uges/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1850.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-D8JE_oE4V0E/T1mBoqWm3mI/AAAAAAAAKs4/q5bsK8-uges/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1850.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               Look how beautiful and "invisible" it looks after the seam is pulled tight! It's nice and flat on the outside.
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-W934O6wOk34/T1mBstRKc6I/AAAAAAAAKtA/_jwcAuaOghg/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1851.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="640" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-W934O6wOk34/T1mBstRKc6I/AAAAAAAAKtA/_jwcAuaOghg/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1851.JPG" width="424" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               Here it is on the reverse--a bit of a bump, but neat.
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-EsKC09TV7v4/T1mBx8dYt6I/AAAAAAAAKtI/ip3QWIMBZIA/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1853.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-EsKC09TV7v4/T1mBx8dYt6I/AAAAAAAAKtI/ip3QWIMBZIA/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1853.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-KECzw--xzg4/T1mB2WQDpEI/AAAAAAAAKtU/I3ypLGSWjMY/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1855.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-KECzw--xzg4/T1mB2WQDpEI/AAAAAAAAKtU/I3ypLGSWjMY/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1855.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               When you have finished stitching your mattress seam you then cut your yarn, leaving a tail and weave in the ends. (I'll post a tutorial on weaving in later.)
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               That is the mattress stitch! I love it!
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
               But now I will show you seaming with a
               <a href="http://www.aestheticnest.com/2012/03/how-to-crochet-4-single-crochet.html">
                single crochet stitch
               </a>
               , which can't be beat for it's simplicity, but it is not as invisible.
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
               SEAMING WITH THE SINGLE CROCHET:
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: left;">
               Unlike the mattress stitch, this seam is created by working with your pieces right sides together. Line up the two pieces to be seamed and use safety pins or stitch markers to hold them together while you work.
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-wnze_l2BCfU/T1mB6IHpXbI/AAAAAAAAKtc/s9kZTrD84pY/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1856.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-wnze_l2BCfU/T1mB6IHpXbI/AAAAAAAAKtc/s9kZTrD84pY/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1856.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/--2WipoO18jM/T1mB_4m6LAI/AAAAAAAAKtk/G1SzNgMVnwE/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1857.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/--2WipoO18jM/T1mB_4m6LAI/AAAAAAAAKtk/G1SzNgMVnwE/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1857.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               Use a crochet hook of the same size as the one used in your pattern, and the same yarn (I'm using a contrasting yarn for ease of viewing). You can leave the yarn attached to the skein.
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-B-P0H9UUukQ/T1mCFLPuIHI/AAAAAAAAKtw/JcZpmO8w-vI/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1858.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-B-P0H9UUukQ/T1mCFLPuIHI/AAAAAAAAKtw/JcZpmO8w-vI/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1858.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               You are going to work a row of
               <a href="http://www.aestheticnest.com/2012/03/how-to-crochet-4-single-crochet.html">
                single crochet
               </a>
               through the two pieces you are seaming by starting in the furthest stitches to the right. Tie a
               <a href="http://www.aestheticnest.com/2012/02/how-to-crochet-1-slip-knot-tutorial.html">
                slip knot
               </a>
               on your hook and insert your hook through the first stitch in each of the pieces you are seaming...
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-3RKFLmYg4Iw/T1mCXK9_VNI/AAAAAAAAKt4/cJAy2mLmWXw/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1860.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-3RKFLmYg4Iw/T1mCXK9_VNI/AAAAAAAAKt4/cJAy2mLmWXw/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1860.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: center;">
               ...and work a single crochetthrough the two pieces just as you would if you were working into a row of single crochet.
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8D5cA-90m2M/T1mCjIQZliI/AAAAAAAAKuM/TEgIGMuFcaI/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1862.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-8D5cA-90m2M/T1mCjIQZliI/AAAAAAAAKuM/TEgIGMuFcaI/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1862.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               Repeat the single crochet stitch working up the seam in each subsequent stitch, or hole. It doesn't really matter into which holes you are working as long as you do it consistently so the single crochet stitches are spaced equally and they're all equally close to the edge of the seam. That wayyour seam will be straight.
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-QAXeFv0K2H8/T1mR9e9eo9I/AAAAAAAAKwQ/mpv2FQE_j74/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1863.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-QAXeFv0K2H8/T1mR9e9eo9I/AAAAAAAAKwQ/mpv2FQE_j74/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1863.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qG_VE1XuirQ/T1mCxw5-0kI/AAAAAAAAKuo/uNVIV4gS2UQ/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1864.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qG_VE1XuirQ/T1mCxw5-0kI/AAAAAAAAKuo/uNVIV4gS2UQ/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1864.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               This is how it will look on the wrong side of the seam.
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-DpTHofcpXxc/T1mC3Li9v9I/AAAAAAAAKuw/ZZafT1bSwH4/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1865.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-DpTHofcpXxc/T1mC3Li9v9I/AAAAAAAAKuw/ZZafT1bSwH4/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1865.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div style="text-align: center;">
               The right side will look like this, however, if you are using the same yarn it will blend in.
              </div>
              <div style="text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-RUSTYpxOnBU/T1mC7k5zq8I/AAAAAAAAKu4/jU9gY4gKBY0/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1866.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-RUSTYpxOnBU/T1mC7k5zq8I/AAAAAAAAKu4/jU9gY4gKBY0/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1866.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               Here is what the single crochet seam looks like if you are using the same yarn to seam. Wrong side:
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-buJJ8cqxbm8/T1mDAdjPMcI/AAAAAAAAKvE/SLaTkIXBf6o/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1867.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-buJJ8cqxbm8/T1mDAdjPMcI/AAAAAAAAKvE/SLaTkIXBf6o/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1867.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-3fvnz64n6NU/T1mDXU3zHPI/AAAAAAAAKvw/50OuawfPlKI/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1871.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-3fvnz64n6NU/T1mDXU3zHPI/AAAAAAAAKvw/50OuawfPlKI/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1871.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               And right side:
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-D_tX-642ExY/T1mDIeaBVUI/AAAAAAAAKvU/9weICC2IscE/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1869.JPG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-D_tX-642ExY/T1mDIeaBVUI/AAAAAAAAKvU/9weICC2IscE/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1869.JPG" width="640" yda="true"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               When you are finished seaming cut yoru yarn leaving a few inches to weave in.
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               And there you have it. Two ways to seam your crochet work.
              </div>
              <div style="border: currentColor;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-UcvK_p6Lp0E/T1kzxYpetmI/AAAAAAAAKrQ/inmXZJfMFm8/s1600/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1872.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                <img border="0" height="424" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-UcvK_p6Lp0E/T1kzxYpetmI/AAAAAAAAKrQ/inmXZJfMFm8/s640/How+to+Seam+Crochet_DSC_1872.jpg" width="640"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               Next up is the double crochet stitch.
              </div>
              <br/>
              <div>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-kYGJpFST5a4/T0lff9qfm9I/AAAAAAAAKSY/sDKOArv395Q/s1600/Head+Over+Heels+in+Crochet_Image_DSC_0868+copy.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0em;">
                <img border="0" lda="true" src="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-kYGJpFST5a4/T0lff9qfm9I/AAAAAAAAKSY/sDKOArv395Q/s800/Head+Over+Heels+in+Crochet_Image_DSC_0868+copy.jpg"/>
               </a>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <i>
                How-to tutorials, patterns, giveaways, reviews and interviews to make certain you are smitten.
               </i>
              </div>
              <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
               <br/>
              </div>
